 Sanjeev Bhatt had sought Amit Shah's role in the Sorabuddin case in the petition besides making him a party in the Supreme Court
 saath hi apane khilaaf do maamalon kii jaanch court kii nigaraanee main SIT se karaane kii maang kii thi
 In its order, the Supreme Court questioned the former IPS Sanjiv Bhatt of Gujarat, the Supreme Court said, the petitioner has no right to choose the investigating agency
 aisa lagata he ki yachikakarta sanjeev bhatta ko raajnneetik partiyon, activist or vested interest group dwaara maamle ke trial ke aakhir main saamne laayaa gaya
